     47 +    gw["YARP routes\n/v1/reports/** ‚Üí settlement"]    
     48 +  end                                                 
     49 +

     51 +    st_api["ReportsController\nGET /v1/reports/*"]    
     52 +    st_domain["Settlement domain\npayouts, cashflows"]
     53 +  end                                                 
     54 +

     56 +    c_openapi["openapi-gateway.yaml\npaths /v1/reports/**"]                                                           
     57 +    c_schemas["schemas/*Report*.json"]                
     58 +  end                                                 
     59 +                                                      
     60 +  ui_dash --> ui_api

      *   *Critical Path:* –í `services/settlement` —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ `/v1/reports/payouts`. –≠–Ω–¥–ø–æ–π–Ω—Ç–∞ `/v1/reports/issuances` –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ –Ω–µ—Ç. **–†–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ:** –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `/v1/reports/issuances` –≤ `IssuanceService` (—Ç–∞–∫ –∫–∞–∫ –æ–Ω –≤–ª–∞–¥–µ–µ—Ç –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏) –∏ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç—å YARP   
  –º–∞—Ä—à—Ä—É—Ç, –ª–∏–±–æ –∞–≥—Ä–µ–≥–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –≤ Settlement (—Å–ª–æ–∂–Ω–µ–µ). –†–µ–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω–¥—É—é –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π –≤–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç –¥–ª—è MVP.                                        
  *   **NX-06 (Schedule):** –¢—Ä–µ–±—É–µ—Ç—Å—è **SPEC DIFF**. –¢–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ –ø–æ–ª–µ `scheduleJson` –≤ `Issuance` ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ tech debt. –í–≤–æ–¥–∏–º —Ç–∏–ø–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç `PayoutScheduleItem` –∏ —ç–Ω–¥–ø–æ–π–Ω—Ç—ã —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —Ä–∞—Å–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º.                                                         
  *   **Infra:** –†–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª—è–µ–º –ø–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥—ã. **UK1** ‚Äî "—Ö—Ä—É—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –ø—Ä–æ–¥", —Ç—Ä–æ–≥–∞–µ–º —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ `docker-compose pull && up -d` –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–æ–≤. **CFA1/Dev** ‚Äî –ø–æ–ª–∏–≥–æ–Ω –¥–ª—è CI/CD –∏ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä—É—à–∞—é—â–∏—Ö —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤.                                                              
  *   **Risks:** –û—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–π —Ä–∏—Å–∫ ‚Äî —Ä–∞—Å—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω –º–µ–∂–¥—É OpenAPI (–≥–¥–µ —ç–Ω–¥–ø–æ–π–Ω—Ç—ã –µ—Å—Ç—å) –∏ YARP/Backend (–≥–¥–µ –∏—Ö –Ω–µ—Ç –∏–ª–∏ –æ–Ω–∏ –≤–µ–¥—É—Ç –≤ –ø—É—Å—Ç–æ—Ç—É).

  ### 2. Detailed Plan                                         

  #### 2.1 NX-05 ‚Äî Issuer Dashboard & Reports                  

  **Why:** –≠–º–∏—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω –≤–∏–¥–µ—Ç—å —Å–≤–æ–¥–∫—É —Å–≤–æ–∏—Ö –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–æ–≤ –∏ –æ–±—è–∑–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤, –∞ –Ω–µ –∑–∞–≥–ª—É—à–∫–∏.                                           
  **What:** Dashboard (KPIs) + Reports Page (Issuances List, Payouts History).                                                 

  **Backend Implementation:**                                  
  1.  **Issuance Service (`services/issuance`):**              
      *   –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `GET /v1/reports/issuances` (–∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç `IssuerIssuancesReportResponse`).                                  
      *   –õ–æ–≥–∏–∫–∞: –ê–≥—Ä–µ–≥–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø–æ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–µ `Issuances` (Count, TotalAmount, SoldAmount ‚Äî –µ—Å–ª–∏ –µ—Å—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –æ –ø—Ä–æ–¥–∞–∂–∞—Ö, –∏–Ω–∞—á–µ mock/TODO).                                                                                                                            
      *   *SPEC DIFF:* –í `openapi-gateway.yaml` —ç—Ç–æ—Ç –ø—É—Ç—å –µ—Å—Ç—å, –Ω–æ YARP —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å —Ä–æ—É—Ç–∏—Ç `/v1/reports/{**catch-all}` –≤ `settlement`.                                                                                                                              
      *   *Action:* –ò–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏—Ç—å `apps/api-gateway/appsettings.json`: –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —è–≤–Ω—ã–π —Ä–æ—É—Ç `/v1/reports/issuances` -> `issuance-service`.                                                                                                                           
  2.  **Settlement Service (`services/settlement`):**          
      *   –î–æ—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç—å `GET /v1/reports/payouts` (—É–∂–µ –µ—Å—Ç—å –≤ `Program.cs`) –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∏ —Ñ–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–æ `issuerId` (—Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å —Ç–∞–º —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –¥–∞—Ç—ã).                                                                                                                      
      *   –£–±–µ–¥–∏—Ç—å—Å—è, —á—Ç–æ `IssuerPayoutsReportResponse` –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—â–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–æ.                                                 

  **Frontend (`apps/portal-issuer`):**                         
  1.  **API Client:**                                          
      *   –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ç—å SDK: `npm run generate` –≤ `packages/sdks/ts`.                                                               
      *   –í `lib/api` –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥—ã: `getIssuerIssuancesReport(params)`, `getPayoutsReport(params)`.                         
      *   –û–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–∏—Ç—å –ø—Ä–æ–±—Ä–æ—Å `x-client-app: portal-issuer` –∏ `traceparent`.                                                    
  2.  **Dashboard Page:**                                      
      *   `Promise.all` –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ KPIs.                         
      *   –ö–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç—ã: `StatCard` (Active Issues, Total Volume), `RecentActivity`.                                              
  3.  **Reports Page:**                                        
      *   Tabs: "Issuances", "Payouts".                        
      *   Table: –ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `shared-ui/DataTable` (–µ—Å–ª–∏ –µ—Å—Ç—å) –∏–ª–∏ Shadcn UI table.                                           
      *   Export: –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å CSV –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—é –Ω–∞ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–µ –∏–∑ JSON-–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö (MVP).                                                   

  **Tests:**                                                   
  *   **E2E (Playwright):** –†–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä–∏—Ç—å `issuer-journey.spec.ts`. –°—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏–π: Login -> Dashboard (–ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞ —Ü–∏—Ñ—Ä != "-") -> Reports (–ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞ –Ω–∞–ª–∏—á–∏—è —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫ –≤ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–µ).                                                                                             

  #### 2.2 NX-06 ‚Äî Issuer Payout Schedule                      

  **Why:** –≠–º–∏—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç—É –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –∑–Ω–∞—Ç—å, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –ø–ª–∞—Ç–∏—Ç—å, –∏ –≤–∏–¥–µ—Ç—å —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å —ç—Ç–∏—Ö –≤—ã–ø–ª–∞—Ç.                                                   
  **What:** UI –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∞ —Ä–∞—Å–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏—è –∏ SPEC DIFF –¥–ª—è —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏–º.                                                         

  **Contracts & SPEC DIFF (Minimal):**                         
  *   **New Endpoints:**                                       
      *   `GET /v1/issuances/{id}/schedule` -> –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—Ç –º–∞—Å—Å–∏–≤–∞ `PayoutScheduleItem` (Date, Amount, Status, PaymentId?).        
      *   `PUT /v1/issuances/{id}/schedule` -> –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ä–∞—Å–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏—è (—Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –¥–ª—è Draft).                                       
  *   **AsyncAPI:**                                            
      *   –ê–∫—Ç—É–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `ois.payout.scheduled`. –î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å payload: `ScheduleId`, `IssuanceId`, `Date`, `Amount`.              
  *   **Domain:**                                              
      *   –í `IssuanceService` –¥–µ—Å–µ—Ä–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `scheduleJson` –≤ —Ç–∏–ø–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—É—é —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—É –¥–ª—è API.                               

  **UI (`apps/portal-issuer`):**                               
  1.  **Issuance Details:** –î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –≤–∫–ª–∞–¥–∫—É "Payout Schedule".
  2.  **Component:** –¢–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `Date | Amount | Status (Scheduled/Pending/Paid)`.                                                
  3.  **Logic:**                                               
      *   Read-only –æ—Ç–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–µ `Issuance.scheduleJson`.                                                             
      *   –°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å –≤—ã—á–∏—Å–ª—è—Ç—å –¥–∏–Ω–∞–º–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏: –µ—Å–ª–∏ –¥–∞—Ç–∞ –ø—Ä–æ—à–ª–∞ –∏ –Ω–µ—Ç —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏—è –≤—ã–ø–ª–∞—Ç—ã ‚Äî "Overdue", –∏–Ω–∞—á–µ "Scheduled".                 

  #### 2.3 Infra Runbooks                                      

  **A. UK1 Runbook (Stable/Demo)**                             
  *   **Role:** Production-like demo. Manual controlled updates.                                                               
  *   **State:** Docker Compose stack (`docker-compose.yml` + `docker-compose.services.yml`).                                  
  *   **Deployment:**                                          
      1.  `ssh user@uk1`                                       
      2.  `cd ois-cfa`                                         
      3.  `git fetch && git checkout <stable-tag-or-branch>` (e.g., `main` or `release/x.y`)                                   
      4.  **Backup:** `bash ops/scripts/backup.sh` (Dump Postgres).                                                            
      5.  `docker-compose pull` (—Ç—è–Ω–µ–º –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑—ã, —Å–æ–±—Ä–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ CI).  
      6.  `docker-compose up -d --remove-orphans` (–ø–µ—Ä–µ–∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫ —Å –Ω–æ–≤—ã–º–∏ –∫–æ–Ω—Ñ–∏–≥–∞–º–∏).                                             
      7.  `make check-health` (smoke test).                    
  *   **Critical Rule:** –ù–µ –º–µ–Ω—è—Ç—å `.env` –∏ `nginx.conf` –±–µ–∑ –±—ç–∫–∞–ø–∞. –ù–µ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç—å –º–∏–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –ª–æ–º–∞—é—â–∏–µ –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω—É—é —Å–æ–≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç—å, –±–µ–∑ –ø–ª–∞–Ω–∞ –æ—Ç–∫–∞—Ç–∞.                                                                                                                 

  **B. CFA1/Dev Runbook (Reproducible)**                       
  *   **Role:** Integration testing, Nightly builds.           
  *   **Setup from Scratch:**                                  
      1.  `apt update && apt install docker.io docker-compose make`                                                            
      2.  `git clone ... ois-cfa`                              
      3.  `cp .env.example .env` (–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç—å –¥–æ–º–µ–Ω `cfa1.example.com`).                                                         
      4.  `bash ops/scripts/setup-certs.sh` (Self-signed –∏–ª–∏ Let's Encrypt).                                                   
      5.  `docker-compose -f docker-compose.yml -f docker-compose.override.dev.yml up -d --build`                              
  *   **Reset Strategy:**                                      
      *   `docker-compose down -v` (–ø–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π —Å–±—Ä–æ—Å –±–∞–∑—ã –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö) —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω –∏ –ø—Ä–∏–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç—Å—è –¥–ª—è —á–∏—Å—Ç—ã—Ö —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤.                     

  #### 2.4 Risk Register                                       

  | Risk | Impact | Location | Mitigation Strategy |           
  | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |                                
  | **YARP Routing Mismatch** | 404 –Ω–∞ —Ä–µ–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞—Ö | `apps/api-gateway/appsettings.json` | –Ø–≤–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–æ–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å —Ä–æ—É—Ç `/v1/reports/issuances` –Ω–∞ `issuance-service`. |                                                                                                   
  | **Issuance 500 Error** | –ü—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª CI/CD | `IssuanceApiTests.cs` | –ü–æ—á–∏–Ω–∏—Ç—å –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫—É `null` –≤ `PublishAsync`. –í–µ—Ä–Ω—É—Ç—å 404 –≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–æ 500. |                                                                                                                      
  | **Missing Producers** | –ù–µ—Ç —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏–π –≤ Kafka | `IssuanceService.cs`, `SettlementService` | –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø—É–±–ª–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—é `ois.payout.scheduled` –ø—Ä–∏ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–∏ –≤—ã–ø—É—Å–∫–∞. |                                                                                            
  | **UK1 Fragility** | –ü—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ–π –¥–µ–º–æ | UK1 Server | –ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `cfa1` –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∏ *–¥–æ* –≤—ã–∫–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ UK1. –ë—ç–∫–∞–ø—ã –ë–î. |          
  | **Schema Validation** | –û—à–∏–±–∫–∏ –≤ CI | `schemas/*.json` | –ò–≥–Ω–æ—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `format: uuid` warnings –≤ AJV –∏–ª–∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å custom formatter –≤ —Ç–µ—Å—Ç—ã. |

‚Ä∫ @tasks/NX-05-issuer-dashboard-and-reports.md @packages/contracts/openapi-gateway.yaml @services/issuance/Program.cs @services/issuance/Services/IssuanceService.cs @apps/api-gateway/appsettings.json @services/settlement/Program.cs                        

  You are a Senior .NET Backend Developer. Your goal is to implement the Backend part of Task NX-05.                           

  Context:                                                     
  - We are implementing "Issuer Dashboard & Reports".          
  - We decided (see NX-05 task) that `GET /v1/reports/issuances` belongs to the **Issuance Service**, while payout reports remain in **Settlement**.                                                                                                           
  - Currently, API Gateway routes ALL `/v1/reports/*` to Settlement. This needs to change.                                     

  Your Mission:                                                

  1.  **Implement `GET /v1/reports/issuances` in `services/issuance`:**                                                        
      -   Create necessary DTOs (`IssuerIssuancesReportResponse`, `IssuerReportRow`) matching `openapi-gateway.yaml`.          
      -   Add the endpoint to `Program.cs` (or a Controller).  
      -   Logic: Query the `Issuances` table by `issuerId` (from query params), filter by date range (optional), and aggregate stats (Total Amount, Status).                                                                                                   
      -   *Note:* For `SoldAmount` and `InvestorsCount`, if you don't have direct access to Registry data yet, return 0 or a mock value with a TODO comment.                                                                                                   

  2.  **Update API Gateway Routing (`apps/api-gateway/appsettings.json`):**                                                    
      -   Add a specific route for `reports-issuances` that matches `/v1/reports/issuances` and forwards it to the `issuance` cluster.                                                                                                                         
      -   **Crucial:** Ensure this route has higher priority (Order) than the generic `reports` route (which forwards to `settlement`).                                                                                                                        

  3.  **Verify Settlement Reports:**                           
      -   Check `services/settlement/Program.cs`. Ensure `GET /v1/reports/payouts` is implemented. If not, add a stub/basic implementation matching the spec.                                                                                                  

  4.  **Verification:**                                        
      -   Build the solution (`dotnet build`).                 
      -   Run `make check-health` (ensure we didn't break basic health).                                                       

  Action:

     67 +        DateOnly? to,                                 
     68 +        CancellationToken ct)                         
     69 +    {                                                 
     70 +        var query = _db.Issuances                     
     71 +            .AsNoTracking()                           
     72 +            .Where(i => i.IssuerId == issuerId);      
     73 +                                                      
     74 +        if (from.HasValue)                            
     75 +        {

     77 +        }                                             
     78 +                                                      
     79 +        if (to.HasValue)                              
     80 +        {                                             
     81 +            query = query.Where(i => i.IssueDate <= to.Value);                                                        
     82 +        }

  builder.Services.AddAuthorization(options =>                 
  {                                                            
      options.AddPolicy("role:issuer", p => p.RequireRole("issuer"));

  .WithName("GetIssuerIssuancesReport")                        
  .RequireAuthorization("role:issuer-or-backoffice")

  ### 4) Settlement Reports –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞                           

  - –í services/settlement/Program.cs —É–∂–µ –µ—Å—Ç—å:                 

  api.MapGet("/reports/payouts", async (                       
      DateOnly? from,                                          
      DateOnly? to,                                            
      ISettlementService service,                              
      CancellationToken ct) =>                                 
  {                                                            
      var fromDate = from ?? DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.UtcNow.AddDays(-30));                                              
      var toDate = to ?? DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.UtcNow);                                                               

      if (fromDate > toDate)                                   
      {                                                        
          return Results.Problem(                              
              detail: "from date must be less than or equal to to date",                                                       
              statusCode: 400,                                 
              title: "Bad Request");                           
      }                                                        

      var result = await service.GetPayoutsReportAsync(fromDate, toDate, ct);                                                  
      return Results.Ok(result);                               
  })                                                           
  .WithName("GetPayoutsReport")

  You are an API Architect and Frontend Dev. Your goal is to complete Task NX-06: Payout Schedule Spec & UI.                   

  Context:                                                     
  - Issuers need to manage payout schedules.                   
  - Currently, backend only has a generic `scheduleJson` field in `Issuance` entity.                                           
  - We follow Spec-First. We need to design the API before implementing the backend logic.                                     

  Your Mission:                                                

  1.  **Design (Spec Diff):**                                  
      -   Create a new file `tasks/NX-06-payout-schedule-SPEC-DIFF.md`.                                                        
      -   Inside this file, define the OpenAPI YAML snippets for:                                                              
          -   `POST /v1/issuances/{id}/payouts/schedule` (Create/Update schedule)                                              
          -   `GET /v1/issuances/{id}/payouts/schedule` (Get schedule)                                                         
          -   `PATCH /v1/issuances/{id}/payouts/schedule/{itemId}` (Update status)                                             
          -   Schema `PayoutScheduleItem`: `{ id: uuid, date: date, amount: decimal, status: "planned"|"paid"|"cancelled" }`.  
      -   Explain that for MVP, the backend might map this to `scheduleJson` JSONB column.                                     

  2.  **Frontend Implementation (Read-Only UI):**              
      -   Modify `apps/portal-issuer/app/issuances/[id]/page.tsx` (Issuance Details).                                          
      -   Add a "Payout Schedule" section or tab.              
      -   It should display data from the existing `scheduleJson` field of the Issuance object (if available).                 
      -   If `scheduleJson` is empty/null, show an empty state.                                                                
      -   Add a "Manage Schedule" button that is **disabled** with a tooltip "Coming soon (Backend API pending)".              

  3.  **Verification:**                                        
      -   Run `npm run build` in `apps/portal-issuer` to ensure no regressions.                                                

  Action:                                                      
  - Create the SPEC DIFF file.                                 
  - Update the React component.                                
  - Verify build.

‚Ä¢ Edited ~/__Repositories/yury-customer/prj_Cifra-rwa-exachange-assets/repositories/customer-gitlab/wt__ois-cfa__NX05/apps/portal-issuer/src/lib/api/issuances.ts (+50 -0)                                                                                     
    20  }                                                      
    21 +                                                       
    22 +export type PayoutScheduleItem = {                     
    23 +  id: string;                                          
    24 +  date: string;                                        
    25 +  amount: number;                                      
    26 +  status: 'planned' | 'paid' | 'cancelled' | string;   
    27 +  note?: string;                                       
    28 +};                                                     
    29 +                                                       
    30 +export function extractScheduleItems(raw: unknown): PayoutScheduleItem[] {                                             
    31 +  if (!raw) return [];                                 
    32 +                                                       
    33 +  const getList = (): unknown[] => {                   
    34 +    if (Array.isArray(raw)) {                          
    35 +      return raw;                                      
    36 +    }                                                  
    37 +                                                       
    38 +    if (typeof raw === 'object') {                     
    39 +      const obj = raw as Record<string, unknown>;      
    40 +      if (Array.isArray(obj.items)) {                  
    41 +        return obj.items;                              
    42 +      }                                                
    43 +      return Object.values(obj);                       
    44 +    }                                                  
    45 +                                                       
    46 +    return [];                                         
    47 +  };                                                   
    48 +                                                       
    49 +  const normalized = getList()                         
    50 +    .filter((item) => typeof item === 'object' && item !== null)                                                       
    51 +    .map((item, idx) => {                              
    52 +      const entry = item as Record<string, unknown>;   
    53 +      return {                                         
    54 +        id: String(entry.id ?? entry.slug ?? idx),     
    55 +        date: typeof entry.date === 'string' ? entry.date : '',                                                        
    56 +        amount:                                        
    57 +          typeof entry.amount === 'number'             
    58 +            ? entry.amount                             
    59 +            : Number(entry.amount ?? 0),               
    60 +        status:                                        
    61 +          typeof entry.status === 'string'             
    62 +            ? entry.status                             
    63 +            : 'planned',                               
    64 +        note: typeof entry.note === 'string' ? entry.note : undefined,                                                 
    65 +      };                                               
    66 +    })                                                 
    67 +    .filter((item) => Boolean(item.date));             
    68 +                                                       
    69 +  return normalized;                                   
    70 +}

    21 +async function call<T>(path: string, init?: RequestInit): Promise<T> {                                                 
    22 +  const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}${path}`, { 
    23 +    ...init,                                           
    24 +    headers: {                                         
    25 +      'Content-Type': 'application/json',              
    26 +      ...(init?.headers ?? {}),                        
    27 +    },                                                 
    28 +    cache: 'no-store',                                 
    29 +  });                                                  
    30 +                                                       
    31 +  if (!response.ok) {                                  
    32 +    throw new Error(`Compliance API error: ${response.status}`);                                                       
    33 +  }                                                    
    34 +                                                       
    35 +  return (await response.json()) as T;

     1 +const API_BASE = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL ?? 'http://localhost:5000';                                      
     2 +                                                       
     3 +export type AuditEvent = {                             
     4 +  id: string;                                          
     5 +  actor: string;                                       
     6 +  action: string;                                      
     7 +  entity: string;                                      
     8 +  timestamp: string;                                   
     9 +  result: 'success' | 'failure' | string;              
    10 +  payload?: Record<string, unknown>;                   
    11 +};                                                     
    12 +                                                       
    13 +export type AuditFilters = {                           
    14 +  from?: string;                                       
    15 +  to?: string;                                         
    16 +  type?: string;                                       
    17 +  actor?: string;                                      
    18 +};                                                     
    19 +                                                       
    20 +async function call<T>(path: string): Promise<T> {     
    21 +  const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}${path}`, { cache: 'no-store' });                                           
    22 +  if (!response.ok) {                                  
    23 +    throw new Error(`Audit API error: ${response.status}`);                                                            
    24 +  }                                                    
    25 +  return (await response.json()) as T;                 
    26 +}                                                      
    27 +                                                       
    28 +export async function getAuditLogs(filters: AuditFilters): Promise<AuditEvent[]> {                                     
    29 +  const query = new URLSearchParams();                 
    30 +  if (filters.from) query.set('from', filters.from);   
    31 +  if (filters.to) query.set('to', filters.to);         
    32 +  if (filters.type) query.set('type', filters.type);   
    33 +  if (filters.actor) query.set('actor', filters.actor);
    34 +                                                       
    35 +  const qs = query.toString();                         
    36 +                                                       
    37 +  try {                                                
    38 +    return await call<AuditEvent[]>(`/v1/audit${qs ? `?${qs}` : ''}`);                                                 
    39 +  } catch {                                            
    40 +    // Temporary mock while backend endpoint stabilizes
    41 +    return [                                           
    42 +      {                                                
    43 +        id: 'mock-audit-1',                            
    44 +        actor: 'backoffice.admin',                     
    45 +        action: 'kyc.approved',                        
    46 +        entity: 'investor#123',                        
    47 +        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),           
    48 +        result: 'success',                             
    49 +        payload: {                                     
    50 +          comment: 'Auto-approve for testing',         
    51 +        },                                             
    52 +      },                                               
    53 +    ];                                                 
    54 +  }

     1 +'use server';                                          
     2 +                                                       
     3 +const API_BASE = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL ?? 'http://localhost:5000';                                      
     4 +                                                       
     5 +async function request<T>(path: string, init?: RequestInit): Promise<T> {                                              
     6 +  const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}${path}`, {      
     7 +    ...init,                                           
     8 +    headers: {                                         
     9 +      'Content-Type': 'application/json',              
    10 +      ...(init?.headers ?? {}),                        
    11 +    },                                                 
    12 +    cache: 'no-store',                                 
    13 +  });                                                  
    14 +                                                       
    15 +  if (!res.ok) {                                       
    16 +    throw new Error(`API error ${res.status}`);        
    17 +  }                                                    
    18 +                                                       
    19 +  if (res.status === 204) {                            
    20 +    return undefined as T;                             
    21 +  }                                                    
    22 +                                                       
    23 +  return (await res.json()) as T;                      
    24 +}                                                      
    25 +                                                       
    26 +export const apiClient = {                             
    27 +  async getAuditEvents(params?: Record<string, string>) {                                                              
    28 +    const search = params ? `?${new URLSearchParams(params).toString()}` : '';                                         
    29 +    try {                                              
    30 +      const data = await request(`/v1/audit${search}`);
    31 +      return { data };                                 
    32 +    } catch {                                          
    33 +      // fallback mock                                 
    34 +      return {                                         
    35 +        data: [                                        
    36 +          {

    51 +        {                                              
    52 +          id: 'doc-demo',                              
    53 +          name: `Document for ${investorId}`,          
    54 +          status: 'uploaded',                          
    55 +        },                                             
    56 +      ],                                               
    57 +    };                                                 
    58 +  },                                                   
    59 +  async makeKycDecision(investorId: string, payload: any) {                                                            
    60 +    await request(`/v1/kyc/${investorId}/decision`, {  
    61 +      method: 'POST',                                  
    62 +      body: JSON.stringify(payload),                   
    63 +    });                                                
    64 +    return { data: { ok: true } };                     
    65 +  },                                                   
    66 +  async uploadKycDocuments() {                         
    67 +    return { data: { ok: true } };                     
    68 +  },                                                   
    69 +  async getInvestorStatus() {                          
    70 +    return { data: { kyc: 'pending' } };               
    71 +  },                                                   
    72 +  async getPayoutsReport(params: { from: string; to: string }) {                                                       
    73 +    const search = `?from=${params.from}&to=${params.to}`;

      5 +  actor: string;                                      
      6 +  actorName?: string;                                 
      7 +  action: string;                                     
      8 +  entity: string;

     15 +};

     17 +export type AuditFilters = {                          
     18 +  from?: string;                                      
     19 +  to?: string;                                        
     20 +  action?: string;                                    
     21 +  actor?: string;                                     
     22 +};                                                    
     23 +                                                      
     24 +const fallbackEvents: AuditEvent[] = [                
     25 +  {                                                   
     26 +    id: 'audit-mock-1',                               
     27 +    actor: 'issuer.portal',                           
     28 +    actorName: 'Issuer Portal',                       
     29 +    action: 'kyc.approve',

     32 +    result: 'success',                                
     33 +    payload: { note: 'Auto-approved for pilot' },     
     34 +  },                                                  
     35 +  {

     44 +];                                                    
     45 +                                                      
     46 +async function callAudit<T>(path: string, init?: RequestInit): Promise<T> {                                           
     47 +  const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}${path}`, {
     48 +    ...init,                                          
     49 +    headers: {                                        
     50 +      'Content-Type': 'application/json',             
     51 +      ...(init?.headers ?? {}),                       
     52 +    },                                                
     53 +    cache: 'no-store',                                
     54 +  });                                                 
     55 +                                                      
     56 +  if (!response.ok) {                                 
     57 +    throw new Error(`Audit API error ${response.status}`);                                                            
     58 +  }                                                   
     59 +                                                      
     60 +  if (response.status === 204) {                      
     61 +    return undefined as T;                            
     62 +  }                                                   
     63 +                                                      
     64 +  return (await response.json()) as T;                
     65 +}                                                     
     66 +                                                      
     67 +function filterFallback(events: AuditEvent[], filters?: AuditFilters): AuditEvent[] {                                 
     68 +  if (!filters) {                                     
     69 +    return events;                                    
     70 +  }                                                   
     71 +                                                      
     72 +  return events.filter((event) => {                   
     73 +    if (filters.action && !event.action.includes(filters.action)) {                                                   
     74 +      return false;                                   
     75 +    }                                                 
     76 +    if (filters.actor && !event.actor.includes(filters.actor)) {                                                      
     77 +      return false;                                   
     78 +    }                                                 
     79 +    if (filters.from && new Date(event.timestamp) < new Date(filters.from)) {                                         
     80 +      return false;                                   
     81 +    }                                                 
     82 +    if (filters.to && new Date(event.timestamp) > new Date(filters.to)) {                                             
     83 +      return false;                                   
     84 +    }                                                 
     85 +    return true;                                      
     86 +  });                                                 
     87 +}                                                     
     88 +                                                      
     89 +export async function getAuditLogs(filters?: AuditFilters): Promise<AuditEvent[]> {                                   
     90 +  const params = new URLSearchParams();               
     91 +  if (filters?.from) params.set('from', filters.from);
     92 +  if (filters?.to) params.set('to', filters.to);      
     93 +  if (filters?.action) params.set('action', filters.action);                                                          
     94 +  if (filters?.actor) params.set('actor', filters.actor);                                                             
     95 +  const search = params.toString() ? `?${params.toString()}` : '';                                                    
     96 +                                                      
     97 +  try {                                               
     98 +    const data = await callAudit<AuditEvent[]>(`/v1/audit${search}`);                                                 
     99 +    return data;                                      
    100 +  } catch {                                           
    101 +    return filterFallback(fallbackEvents, filters);   
    102 +  }                                                   
    103 +}                                                     
    104 +                                                      
    105 +export async function getAuditEvent(id: string): Promise<AuditEvent | null> {                                         
    106 +  try {                                               
    107 +    return await callAudit<AuditEvent>(`/v1/audit/${id}`);                                                            
    108 +  } catch {                                           
    109 +    const logs = await getAuditLogs();                
    110 +    return logs.find((event) => event.id === id) ?? null;                                                             
    111 +  }                                                   
    112 +}

    28 +                                                       
    29 +async function callReports<T>(path: string, init?: RequestInit): Promise<T> {                                          
    30 +  const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}${path}`, { 
    31 +    ...init,                                           
    32 +    headers: {                                         
    33 +      'Content-Type': 'application/json',              
    34 +      ...(init?.headers ?? {}),                        
    35 +    },                                                 
    36 +    cache: 'no-store',                                 
    37 +  });                                                  
    38 +                                                       
    39 +  if (!response.ok) {                                  
    40 +    throw new Error(`Reports API error ${response.status}`);                                                           
    41 +  }                                                    
    42 +

    44 +    return undefined as T;

    49 +                                                       
    50 +export async function getPayoutsReport(params: { from: string; to: string }): Promise<PayoutReport> {                  
    51 +  const search = new URLSearchParams({ from: params.from, to: params.to });                                            
    52 +                                                       
    53 +  try {                                                
    54 +    const data = await callReports<PayoutReport>(`/v1/reports/payouts?${search.toString()}`);                          
    55 +    return {                                           
    56 +      totalAmount: data.totalAmount ?? data.items?.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.amount ?? 0), 0) ?? 0,            
    57 +      totalItems: data.totalItems ?? data.items?.length ?? 0,                                                          
    58 +      items: data.items ?? [],                         
    59 +    };                                                 
    60 +  } catch {                                            
    61 +    return FALLBACK_REPORT;                            
    62 +  }                                                    
    63 +}                                                      
    64 +                                                       
    65 +export async function runSettlement(params?: { date?: string }): Promise<SettlementJob> {

    67 +                                                       
    68 +  try {                                                
    69 +    return await callReports<SettlementJob>(`/v1/settlement/run${search}`, {                                           
    70 +      method: 'POST',                                  
    71 +    });                                                
    72 +  } catch {                                            
    73 +    return { status: 'queued', referenceId: 'mock-job' };                                                              
    74 +  }                                                    
    75 +}

     10 +  { label: 'All actions', value: '' },                
     11 +  { label: 'KYC', value: 'kyc' },                     
     12 +  { label: 'Auth', value: 'login' },                  
     13 +  { label: 'Issuance', value: 'issuance' },           
     14 +];                                                    
     15 +                                                      
     16 +export default function AuditPage() {                 
     17 +  const [from, setFrom] = useState('');               
     18 +  const [to, setTo] = useState('');                   
     19 +  const [action, setAction] = useState('');           
     20 +  const [actor, setActor] = useState('');             
     21 +  const [selectedEvent, setSelectedEvent] = useState<AuditEvent | null>(null);                                        
     22 +                                                      
     23 +  const filters = useMemo<AuditFilters>(              
     24 +    () => ({                                          
     25 +      from: from || undefined,                        
     26 +      to: to || undefined,                            
     27 +      action: action || undefined,                    
     28 +      actor: actor || undefined,                      
     29 +    }),                                               
     30 +    [from, to, action, actor],                        
     31 +  );                                                  
     32 +                                                      
     33 +  const {                                             
     34 +    data: events = [],                                
     35 +    isLoading,                                        
     36 +    refetch,                                          
     37 +  } = useQuery({                                      
     38 +    queryKey: ['audit-logs', filters],                
     39 +    queryFn: () => getAuditLogs(filters),             
     40 +  });                                                 
     41 +                                                      
     42 +  const resetFilters = () => {                        
     43 +    setFrom('');                                      
     44 +    setTo('');                                        
     45 +    setAction('');                                    
     46 +    setActor('');                                     
     47 +    setSelectedEvent(null);                           
     48 +    refetch();                                        
     49 +  };                                                  
     50 +                                                      
     51 +  return (                                            
     52 +    <main className="mx-auto max-w-6xl space-y-8 px-6 py-10">                                                         
     53 +      <header className="space-y-2">                  
     54 +        <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Audit Explorer</p>                                                       
     55 +        <h1 className="text-3xl font-semibold text-gray-900">Audit Log</h1>                                           
     56 +        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">         
     57 +          Inspect issuer/backoffice actions. Filters are applied at API level with mock fallback when backend         
     58 +          –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–µ–Ω.                                 
     59 +        </p>                                          
     60 +      </header>                                       
     61 +                                                      
     62 +      <section className="rounded-xl border border-gray-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">                                  
     63 +        <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-4">   
     64 +          <label className="flex flex-col gap-1 text-sm text-gray-600">                                               
     65 +            From                                      
     66 +            <input                                    
     67 +              type="date"                             
     68 +              value={from}                            
     69 +              onChange={(event) => setFrom(event.target.value)}                                                       
     70 +              className="rounded-md border border-gray-300 px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 focus:border-blue-500 focus:outline-none"                                                                                                                          
     71 +            />                                        
     72 +          </label>                                    
     73 +          <label className="flex flex-col gap-1 text-sm text-gray-600">                                               
     74 +            To                                        
     75 +            <input                                    
     76 +              type="date"                             
     77 +              value={to}                              
     78 +              onChange={(event) => setTo(event.target.value)}                                                         
     79 +              className="rounded-md border border-gray-300 px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 focus:border-blue-500 focus:outline-none"                                                                                                                          
     80 +            />                                        
     81 +          </label>                                    
     82 +          <label className="flex flex-col gap-1 text-sm text-gray-600">                                               
     83 +            Action                                    
     84 +            <select                                   
     85 +              value={action}                          
     86 +              onChange={(event) => setAction(event.target.value)}                                                     
     87 +              className="rounded-md border border-gray-300 px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 focus:border-blue-500 focus:outline-none"                                                                                                                          
     88 +            >                                         
     89 +              {actionOptions.map((option) => (        
     90 +                <option key={option.value} value={option.value}>                                                      
     91 +                  {option.label}                      
     92 +                </option>                             
     93 +              ))}                                     
     94 +            </select>                                 
     95 +          </label>                                    
     96 +          <label className="flex flex-col gap-1 text-sm text-gray-600">                                               
     97 +            Actor                                     
     98 +            <input                                    
     99 +              type="text"                             
    100 +              value={actor}                           
    101 +              placeholder="issuer.portal"             
    102 +              onChange={(event) => setActor(event.target.value)}                                                      
    103 +              className="rounded-md border border-gray-300 px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 focus:border-blue-500 focus:outline-none"                                                                                                                          
    104 +            />                                        
    105 +          </label>                                    
    106 +        </div>                                        
    107 +        <div className="mt-4 flex items-center gap-3">
    108 +          <button                                     
    109 +            type="button"                             
    110 +            onClick={() => refetch()}                 
    111 +            className="rounded-md bg-blue-600 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white hover:bg-blue-700 disabled:opacity-50"                                                                                                                         
    112 +            disabled={isLoading}                      
    113 +          >                                           
    114 +            Apply Filters                             
    115 +          </button>                                   
    116 +          <button                                     
    117 +            type="button"                             
    118 +            onClick={resetFilters}                    
    119 +            className="rounded-md border border-gray-300 px-4 py-2 text-sm text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-50"            
    120 +          >                                           
    121 +            Reset                                     
    122 +          </button>                                   
    123 +        </div>                                        
    124 +      </section>                                      
    125 +                                                      
    126 +      <section className="rounded-xl border border-gray-200 bg-white shadow-sm">                                      
    127 +        <div className="overflow-x-auto">             
    128 +          <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200 text-sm">                                             
    129 +            <thead className="bg-gray-50 text-left text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-gray-500">     
    130 +              <tr>                                    
    131 +                <th className="px-4 py-3">Timestamp</th>                                                              
    132 +                <th className="px-4 py-3">Actor</th>  
    133 +                <th className="px-4 py-3">Action</th> 
    134 +                <th className="px-4 py-3">Entity</th> 
    135 +                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right">Status</th>                                                      
    136 +              </tr>                                   
    137 +            </thead>                                  
    138 +            <tbody className="divide-y divide-gray-100">                                                              
    139 +              {isLoading && (                         
    140 +                <tr>                                  
    141 +                  <td colSpan={5} className="px-4 py-6 text-center text-gray-500">                                    
    142 +                    Loading audit events‚Ä¶             
    143 +                  </td>                               
    144 +                </tr>                                 
    145 +              )}                                      
    146 +              {!isLoading && events.length === 0 && ( 
    147 +                <tr>                                  
    148 +                  <td colSpan={5} className="px-4 py-6 text-center text-gray-400">                                    
    149 +                    No events for selected filters.   
    150 +                  </td>                               
    151 +                </tr>                                 
    152 +              )}                                      
    153 +              {events.map((event) => (                
    154 +                <tr key={event.id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">                                                      
    155 +                  <td className="px-4 py-3 align-top text-sm text-gray-900">                                          
    156 +                    {new Date(event.timestamp).toLocaleString()}                                                      
    157 +                  </td>                               
    158 +                  <td className="px-4 py-3">          
    159 +                    <div className="font-medium text-gray-900">{event.actorName ?? event.actor}</div>                 
    160 +                    {event.ip && <div className="text-xs text-gray-500">{event.ip}</div>}                             
    161 +                  </td>                               
    162 +                  <td className="px-4 py-3 text-gray-800">                                                            
    163 +                    <div className="font-medium">{event.action}</div>                                                 
    164 +                    {event.payload && (               
    165 +                      <button                         
    166 +                        type="button"                 
    167 +                        className="text-xs text-blue-600 hover:underline"                                             
    168 +                        onClick={() => setSelectedEvent(event)}                                                       
    169 +                      >                               
    170 +                        View payload                  
    171 +                      </button>                       
    172 +                    )}                                
    173 +                  </td>                               
    174 +                  <td className="px-4 py-3 text-gray-700">                                                            
    175 +                    <div>{event.entity}</div>         
    176 +                    {event.entityId && <div className="text-xs text-gray-500">{event.entityId}</div>}                 
    177 +                  </td>                               
    178 +                  <td className="px-4 py-3">          
    179 +                    <div className="flex flex-col items-end gap-2 text-sm">                                           
    180 +                      <span className="rounded-full bg-gray-100 px-2 py-0.5 text-xs capitalize text-gray-700">        
    181 +                        {event.result ?? 'pending'}   
    182 +                      </span>                         
    183 +                      <Link href={`/audit/${event.id}`} className="text-xs font-medium text-blue-600 hover:underline">
    184 +                        Details                       
    185 +                      </Link>                         
    186 +                    </div>                            
    187 +                  </td>                               
    188 +                </tr>                                 
    189 +              ))}                                     
    190 +            </tbody>                                  
    191 +          </table>                                    
    192 +        </div>                                        
    193 +      </section>                                      
    194 +                                                      
    195 +      {selectedEvent && (                             
    196 +        <section className="rounded-xl border border-blue-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">                                
    197 +          <div className="flex items-start justify-between">                                                          
    198 +            <div>                                     
    199 +              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Payload preview</p>                                                
    200 +              <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900">{selectedEvent.action}</h2>                         
    201 +              <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">   
    202 +                Event ID: <span className="font-mono">{selectedEvent.id}</span>                                       
    203 +              </p>                                    
    204 +            </div>                                    
    205 +            <button                                   
    206 +              type="button"                           
    207 +              className="text-sm text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700"                                                   
    208 +              onClick={() => setSelectedEvent(null)}  
    209 +            >                                         
    210 +              Close                                   
    211 +            </button>                                 
    212 +          </div>                                      
    213 +          <pre className="mt-4 max-h-64 overflow-auto rounded-lg bg-gray-900 p-4 text-xs text-green-200">             
    214 +            {JSON.stringify(selectedEvent.payload ?? {}, null, 2)}                                                    
    215 +          </pre>                                      
    216 +        </section>                                    
    217 +      )}                                              
    218 +    </main>                                           
    219 +  );                                                  
    220 +}

‚Ä∫ –°–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏, —è –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª —Ñ–∞–π–ª, –∞–≥–µ–Ω—Ç –ø–æ–¥—É–º–∞–ª –∏ –ø—Ä–æ—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–ª. –í–æ—Ç –æ–Ω —Ç–µ–±–µ –¥–∞–ª —Ñ–∏–¥–±—ç–∫: –Ω–∞—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –æ–Ω –≥–ª—É–±–æ–∫–∏–π, –≤—Å—ë –ª–∏ —Ç–µ–±–µ –ø–æ–Ω—è—Ç–Ω–æ, –µ—Å—Ç—å –ª–∏ —É —Ç–µ–±—è –≤–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å—ã, –µ—Å—Ç—å –ª–∏ —Å —á–µ–º-—Ç–æ —Ç—ã —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–µ–Ω, –Ω–µ —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–µ–Ω? –¢—ã —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –∂–µ player-–ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–µ—Ä, —Å–µ–Ω—å–æ—Ä, –º–æ–∂–µ—à—å –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ-—Ç–æ –≤–µ—â–∏ —Ç—É—Ç. 

  –ï—Å–ª–∏ —É —Ç–µ–±—è –≤—Å—ë –ø–æ–Ω—è—Ç–Ω–æ, —Ç–æ —Ç–æ–≥–¥–∞ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —ç—Ç–æ –≤ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–µ –≤–µ–∑–¥–µ –æ—Ç—Ä–∞–∑–∏—Ç—å: –∏ deliverables, –∏ kick-off-task, –Ω—É —Ç–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å definition of data. –ò –∫–∞–∫ –±—ã –¥–≤–∏–≥–∞—Ç—å—Å—è, —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å —ç—Ç–æ –∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ, –≤—Å—ë –ø–æ –ø–ª–∞–Ω—É, —Å–æ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–æ–π, –Ω–∏—á–µ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –ª–æ–º–∞—è.                         

  –í–æ—Ç, –ø–æ –ø–æ–≤–æ–¥—É —Ç–æ–≥–æ, —á—Ç–æ —è –≤–∏–∂—É: EK1 runbook, —Ç—É—Ç –±—É–¥–µ—Ç, –∫–æ–Ω–µ—á–Ω–æ, –Ω–µ–±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–π –∞–ø–¥–µ–π—Ç. –¢–æ, —á—Ç–æ –º—ã –±—É–¥–µ–º –ø–æ–¥–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ç—å stable demo, –¥–∞, –≤ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø–µ, –≤—Å—ë –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ —Ç—É—Ç –¥–∞–∂–µ –Ω–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–æ.                                                                                 

  –ù—É –¥–∞–≤–∞–π, –ø—É—Å—Ç—å —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å. –ï–¥–∏–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–µ, –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç—å –Ω–µ—É—Ç–æ–º–∏–º–æ until job to be done: —Ö–æ—Ç—å 30 –º–∏–Ω—É—Ç, —Ö–æ—Ç—å —á–∞—Å, —Ö–æ—Ç—å –¥–≤–∞.                                                                                                                               

  –ü—Ä–∏–≤–µ—Ç. –Ø –∏–∑—É—á–∏–ª –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∞—Ä—Ç–µ—Ñ–∞–∫—Ç—ã, –≤–∫–ª—é—á–∞—è –Ω–æ–≤—É—é —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—é NX-05, –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç NX-06 –∏ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ –∏–Ω—Ñ—Ä–∞—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—ã.     

  –ù–∏–∂–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω –¥–µ—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –ø–ª–∞–Ω —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∏ –∞—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç—É—Ä–Ω—ã–π —Ä–∞–∑–±–æ—Ä –¥–ª—è –¥–≤–∏–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫ –¥–µ–º–æ.                                       

  ### 1. TL;DR                                                 

  *   **NX-05 (Reports):** –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–≥–æ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ **TS SDK** –∏ **API Gateway**.                                               
      *   *Critical Path:* –í `services/settlement` —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ `/v1/reports/payouts`. –≠–Ω–¥–ø–æ–π–Ω—Ç–∞ `/v1/reports/issuances` –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ –Ω–µ—Ç. **–†–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ:** –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `/v1/reports/issuances` –≤ `IssuanceService` (—Ç–∞–∫ –∫–∞–∫ –æ–Ω –≤–ª–∞–¥–µ–µ—Ç –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏) –∏ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç—å YARP   
  –º–∞—Ä—à—Ä—É—Ç, –ª–∏–±–æ –∞–≥—Ä–µ–≥–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –≤ Settlement (—Å–ª–æ–∂–Ω–µ–µ). –†–µ–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω–¥—É—é –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π –≤–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç –¥–ª—è MVP.                                        
  *   **NX-06 (Schedule):** –¢—Ä–µ–±—É–µ—Ç—Å—è **SPEC DIFF**. –¢–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ –ø–æ–ª–µ `scheduleJson` –≤ `Issuance` ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ tech debt. –í–≤–æ–¥–∏–º —Ç–∏–ø–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç `PayoutScheduleItem` –∏ —ç–Ω–¥–ø–æ–π–Ω—Ç—ã —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —Ä–∞—Å–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º.                                                         
  *   **Infra:** –†–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª—è–µ–º –ø–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥—ã. **UK1** ‚Äî "—Ö—Ä—É—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –ø—Ä–æ–¥", —Ç—Ä–æ–≥–∞–µ–º —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ `docker-compose pull && up -d` –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–æ–≤. **CFA1/Dev** ‚Äî –ø–æ–ª–∏–≥–æ–Ω –¥–ª—è CI/CD –∏ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä—É—à–∞—é—â–∏—Ö —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤.                                                              
  *   **Risks:** –û—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–π —Ä–∏—Å–∫ ‚Äî —Ä–∞—Å—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω –º–µ–∂–¥—É OpenAPI (–≥–¥–µ —ç–Ω–¥–ø–æ–π–Ω—Ç—ã –µ—Å—Ç—å) –∏ YARP/Backend (–≥–¥–µ –∏—Ö –Ω–µ—Ç –∏–ª–∏ –æ–Ω–∏ –≤–µ–¥—É—Ç –≤ –ø—É—Å—Ç–æ—Ç—É).                                                                                                                            

  ---                                                          

  ### 2. Detailed Plan                                         

  #### 2.1 NX-05 ‚Äî Issuer Dashboard & Reports                  

  **Why:** –≠–º–∏—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω –≤–∏–¥–µ—Ç—å —Å–≤–æ–¥–∫—É —Å–≤–æ–∏—Ö –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–æ–≤ –∏ –æ–±—è–∑–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤, –∞ –Ω–µ –∑–∞–≥–ª—É—à–∫–∏.                                           
  **What:** Dashboard (KPIs) + Reports Page (Issuances List, Payouts History).                                                 

  **Backend Implementation:**                                  
  1.  **Issuance Service (`services/issuance`):**              
      *   –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `GET /v1/reports/issuances` (–∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç `IssuerIssuancesReportResponse`).                                  
      *   –õ–æ–≥–∏–∫–∞: –ê–≥—Ä–µ–≥–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø–æ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–µ `Issuances` (Count, TotalAmount, SoldAmount ‚Äî –µ—Å–ª–∏ –µ—Å—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –æ –ø—Ä–æ–¥–∞–∂–∞—Ö, –∏–Ω–∞—á–µ mock/TODO).                                                                                                                            
      *   *SPEC DIFF:* –í `openapi-gateway.yaml` —ç—Ç–æ—Ç –ø—É—Ç—å –µ—Å—Ç—å, –Ω–æ YARP —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å —Ä–æ—É—Ç–∏—Ç `/v1/reports/{**catch-all}` –≤ `settlement`.                                                                                                                              
      *   *Action:* –ò–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏—Ç—å `apps/api-gateway/appsettings.json`: –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —è–≤–Ω—ã–π —Ä–æ—É—Ç `/v1/reports/issuances` -> `issuance-service`.                                                                                                                           
  2.  **Settlement Service (`services/settlement`):**          
      *   –î–æ—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç—å `GET /v1/reports/payouts` (—É–∂–µ –µ—Å—Ç—å –≤ `Program.cs`) –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∏ —Ñ–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–æ `issuerId` (—Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å —Ç–∞–º —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –¥–∞—Ç—ã).                                                                                                                      
      *   –£–±–µ–¥–∏—Ç—å—Å—è, —á—Ç–æ `IssuerPayoutsReportResponse` –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—â–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–æ.                                                 

  **Frontend (`apps/portal-issuer`):**                         
  1.  **API Client:**                                          
      *   –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ç—å SDK: `npm run generate` –≤ `packages/sdks/ts`.                                                               
      *   –í `lib/api` –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥—ã: `getIssuerIssuancesReport(params)`, `getPayoutsReport(params)`.                         
      *   –û–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–∏—Ç—å –ø—Ä–æ–±—Ä–æ—Å `x-client-app: portal-issuer` –∏ `traceparent`.                                                    
  2.  **Dashboard Page:**                                      
      *   `Promise.all` –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ KPIs.                         
      *   –ö–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç—ã: `StatCard` (Active Issues, Total Volume), `RecentActivity`.                                              
  3.  **Reports Page:**                                        
      *   Tabs: "Issuances", "Payouts".                        
      *   Table: –ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `shared-ui/DataTable` (–µ—Å–ª–∏ –µ—Å—Ç—å) –∏–ª–∏ Shadcn UI table.                                           
      *   Export: –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å CSV –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—é –Ω–∞ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–µ –∏–∑ JSON-–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö (MVP).                                                   

  **Tests:**                                                   
  *   **E2E (Playwright):** –†–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä–∏—Ç—å `issuer-journey.spec.ts`. –°—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏–π: Login -> Dashboard (–ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞ —Ü–∏—Ñ—Ä != "-") -> Reports (–ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞ –Ω–∞–ª–∏—á–∏—è —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫ –≤ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–µ).                                                                                             

  #### 2.2 NX-06 ‚Äî Issuer Payout Schedule                      

  **Why:** –≠–º–∏—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç—É –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –∑–Ω–∞—Ç—å, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –ø–ª–∞—Ç–∏—Ç—å, –∏ –≤–∏–¥–µ—Ç—å —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å —ç—Ç–∏—Ö –≤—ã–ø–ª–∞—Ç.                                                   
  **What:** UI –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∞ —Ä–∞—Å–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏—è –∏ SPEC DIFF –¥–ª—è —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏–º.                                                         

  **Contracts & SPEC DIFF (Minimal):**                         
  *   **New Endpoints:**                                       
      *   `GET /v1/issuances/{id}/schedule` -> –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—Ç –º–∞—Å—Å–∏–≤–∞ `PayoutScheduleItem` (Date, Amount, Status, PaymentId?).        
      *   `PUT /v1/issuances/{id}/schedule` -> –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ä–∞—Å–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏—è (—Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –¥–ª—è Draft).                                       
  *   **AsyncAPI:**                                            
      *   –ê–∫—Ç—É–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `ois.payout.scheduled`. –î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å payload: `ScheduleId`, `IssuanceId`, `Date`, `Amount`.              
  *   **Domain:**                                              
      *   –í `IssuanceService` –¥–µ—Å–µ—Ä–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `scheduleJson` –≤ —Ç–∏–ø–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—É—é —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—É –¥–ª—è API.                               

  **UI (`apps/portal-issuer`):**                               
  1.  **Issuance Details:** –î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –≤–∫–ª–∞–¥–∫—É "Payout Schedule".
  2.  **Component:** –¢–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü–∞ `Date | Amount | Status (Scheduled/Pending/Paid)`.                                                
  3.  **Logic:**                                               
      *   Read-only –æ—Ç–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–µ `Issuance.scheduleJson`.                                                             
      *   –°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å –≤—ã—á–∏—Å–ª—è—Ç—å –¥–∏–Ω–∞–º–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏: –µ—Å–ª–∏ –¥–∞—Ç–∞ –ø—Ä–æ—à–ª–∞ –∏ –Ω–µ—Ç —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏—è –≤—ã–ø–ª–∞—Ç—ã ‚Äî "Overdue", –∏–Ω–∞—á–µ "Scheduled".                 

  #### 2.3 Infra Runbooks                                      

  **A. UK1 Runbook (Stable/Demo)**                             
  *   **Role:** Production-like demo. Manual controlled updates.                                                               
  *   **State:** Docker Compose stack (`docker-compose.yml` + `docker-compose.services.yml`).                                  
  *   **Deployment:**                                          
      1.  `ssh user@uk1`                                       
      2.  `cd ois-cfa`                                         
      3.  `git fetch && git checkout <stable-tag-or-branch>` (e.g., `main` or `release/x.y`)                                   
      4.  **Backup:** `bash ops/scripts/backup.sh` (Dump Postgres).                                                            
      5.  `docker-compose pull` (—Ç—è–Ω–µ–º –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑—ã, —Å–æ–±—Ä–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ CI).  
      6.  `docker-compose up -d --remove-orphans` (–ø–µ—Ä–µ–∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫ —Å –Ω–æ–≤—ã–º–∏ –∫–æ–Ω—Ñ–∏–≥–∞–º–∏).                                             
      7.  `make check-health` (smoke test).                    
  *   **Critical Rule:** –ù–µ –º–µ–Ω—è—Ç—å `.env` –∏ `nginx.conf` –±–µ–∑ –±—ç–∫–∞–ø–∞. –ù–µ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç—å –º–∏–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –ª–æ–º–∞—é—â–∏–µ –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω—É—é —Å–æ–≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç—å, –±–µ–∑ –ø–ª–∞–Ω–∞ –æ—Ç–∫–∞—Ç–∞.                                                                                                                 

  **B. CFA1/Dev Runbook (Reproducible)**                       
  *   **Role:** Integration testing, Nightly builds.           
  *   **Setup from Scratch:**                                  
      1.  `apt update && apt install docker.io docker-compose make`                                                            
      2.  `git clone ... ois-cfa`                              
      3.  `cp .env.example .env` (–Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç—å –¥–æ–º–µ–Ω `cfa1.example.com`).                                                         
      4.  `bash ops/scripts/setup-certs.sh` (Self-signed –∏–ª–∏ Let's Encrypt).                                                   
      5.  `docker-compose -f docker-compose.yml -f docker-compose.override.dev.yml up -d --build`                              
  *   **Reset Strategy:**                                      
      *   `docker-compose down -v` (–ø–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π —Å–±—Ä–æ—Å –±–∞–∑—ã –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö) —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω –∏ –ø—Ä–∏–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç—Å—è –¥–ª—è —á–∏—Å—Ç—ã—Ö —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤.                     

  #### 2.4 Risk Register                                       

  | Risk | Impact | Location | Mitigation Strategy |           
  | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |                                
  | **YARP Routing Mismatch** | 404 –Ω–∞ —Ä–µ–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞—Ö | `apps/api-gateway/appsettings.json` | –Ø–≤–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–æ–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å —Ä–æ—É—Ç `/v1/reports/issuances` –Ω–∞ `issuance-service`. |                                                                                                   
  | **Issuance 500 Error** | –ü—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª CI/CD | `IssuanceApiTests.cs` | –ü–æ—á–∏–Ω–∏—Ç—å –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫—É `null` –≤ `PublishAsync`. –í–µ—Ä–Ω—É—Ç—å 404 –≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–æ 500. |                                                                                                                      
  | **Missing Producers** | –ù–µ—Ç —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏–π –≤ Kafka | `IssuanceService.cs`, `SettlementService` | –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø—É–±–ª–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—é `ois.payout.scheduled` –ø—Ä–∏ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–∏ –≤—ã–ø—É—Å–∫–∞. |                                                                                            
  | **UK1 Fragility** | –ü—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ–π –¥–µ–º–æ | UK1 Server | –ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `cfa1` –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∏ *–¥–æ* –≤—ã–∫–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ UK1. –ë—ç–∫–∞–ø—ã –ë–î. |          
  | **Schema Validation** | –û—à–∏–±–∫–∏ –≤ CI | `schemas/*.json` | –ò–≥–Ω–æ—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å `format: uuid` warnings –≤ AJV –∏–ª–∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å custom formatter –≤ —Ç–µ—Å—Ç—ã. |

  ### 3. Tables: Feature Mapping & Verification                

  **NX-05/06 Implementation Matrix**                           

  | Feature | Endpoint | Target Service | Frontend Route | Test Coverage Required |                                            
  | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |                         
  | **Issuer Dashboard** | `GET /v1/reports/issuances` | `Issuance` (via GW) | `/dashboard` | Unit (Svc), E2E (Render) |       
  | **Issuances Report** | `GET /v1/reports/issuances` | `Issuance` (via GW) | `/reports?tab=issuances` | E2E (Filter/Sort) |  
  | **Payouts Report** | `GET /v1/reports/payouts` | `Settlement` | `/reports?tab=payouts` | Integration (API) |               
  | **Payout Schedule** | `GET /v1/issuances/{id}` | `Issuance` | `/issuances/[id]` | Component (Table) |                      

  **Runbook Verification Steps**                               

  | Step | Command | Expected Output |                         
  | :--- | :--- | :--- |                                       
  | **1. Gateway Health** | `curl -I http://localhost:5000/health` | `HTTP/1.1 200 OK` |                                       
  | **2. Service Routing** | `curl http://localhost:5000/v1/issuances` | `401 Unauthorized` (–∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç —Ä–æ—É—Ç–∏–Ω–≥ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç, auth —Ç–æ–∂–µ) |                                                                                                                             
  | **3. Reports API** | `curl -H "Auth..." http://localhost:5000/v1/reports/issuances` | JSON list/summary (–Ω–µ 404/502) |     
  | **4. Frontend Assets** | `curl -I http://localhost:3001` | `HTTP/1.1 200 OK` (Next.js response) |                          

  ---

‚Ä∫ @tasks/NX-05-issuer-dashboard-and-reports.md @packages/contracts/openapi-gateway.yaml @services/issuance/Program.cs @services/issuance/Services/IssuanceService.cs @apps/api-gateway/appsettings.json @services/settlement/Program.cs                        

  You are a Senior .NET Backend Developer. Your goal is to implement the Backend part of Task NX-05.                           

  Context:                                                     
  - We are implementing "Issuer Dashboard & Reports".          
  - We decided (see NX-05 task) that `GET /v1/reports/issuances` belongs to the **Issuance Service**, while payout reports remain in **Settlement**.                                                                                                           
  - Currently, API Gateway routes ALL `/v1/reports/*` to Settlement. This needs to change.                                     

  Your Mission:                                                

  1.  **Implement `GET /v1/reports/issuances` in `services/issuance`:**                                                        
      -   Create necessary DTOs (`IssuerIssuancesReportResponse`, `IssuerReportRow`) matching `openapi-gateway.yaml`.          
      -   Add the endpoint to `Program.cs` (or a Controller).  
      -   Logic: Query the `Issuances` table by `issuerId` (from query params), filter by date range (optional), and aggregate stats (Total Amount, Status).                                                                                                   
      -   *Note:* For `SoldAmount` and `InvestorsCount`, if you don't have direct access to Registry data yet, return 0 or a mock value with a TODO comment.                                                                                                   

  2.  **Update API Gateway Routing (`apps/api-gateway/appsettings.json`):**                                                    
      -   Add a specific route for `reports-issuances` that matches `/v1/reports/issuances` and forwards it to the `issuance` cluster.                                                                                                                         
      -   **Crucial:** Ensure this route has higher priority (Order) than the generic `reports` route (which forwards to `settlement`).                                                                                                                        

  3.  **Verify Settlement Reports:**                           
      -   Check `services/settlement/Program.cs`. Ensure `GET /v1/reports/payouts` is implemented. If not, add a stub/basic implementation matching the spec.                                                                                                  

  4.  **Verification:**                                        
      -   Build the solution (`dotnet build`).                 
      -   Run `make check-health` (ensure we didn't break basic health).                                                       

  Action:                                                      
  - Modify the code.                                           
  - Verify compilation.
