  ### 4) Settlement Reports –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞                           

  - –í services/settlement/Program.cs —É–∂–µ –µ—Å—Ç—å:                 

  api.MapGet("/reports/payouts", async (                       
      DateOnly? from,                                          
      DateOnly? to,                                            
      ISettlementService service,                              
      CancellationToken ct) =>                                 
  {                                                            
      var fromDate = from ?? DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.UtcNow.AddDays(-30));                                              
      var toDate = to ?? DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.UtcNow);                                                               

      if (fromDate > toDate)                                   
      {                                                        
          return Results.Problem(                              
              detail: "from date must be less than or equal to to date",                                                       
              statusCode: 400,                                 
              title: "Bad Request");                           
      }                                                        

      var result = await service.GetPayoutsReportAsync(fromDate, toDate, ct);                                                  
      return Results.Ok(result);                               
  })                                                           
  .WithName("GetPayoutsReport")                                
  .RequireAuthorization("role:issuer-or-backoffice")           
  .WithOpenApi();                                              

  - –í services/settlement/Services/SettlementService.cs —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è GetPayoutsReportAsync —É–∂–µ —Å–æ–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç PayoutsReportResponse (–∞–≥—Ä–µ–≥–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø–æ PayoutBatches –∏ PayoutItems).

‚Ä¢ TL;DR                                                        

  - IIssuanceService.PublishAsync/CloseAsync now return null instead of throwing when an issuance is missing, so HTTP handlers can answer 404s cleanly (services/issuance/Services/IssuanceService.cs:8).                                                      
  - /v1/issuances/{id}/publish|close endpoints rely on that nullable result, eliminating the double-lookup race and keeping other validation (status checks) intact (services/issuance/Program.cs:228).                                                        
  - Couldn‚Äôt execute dotnet test locally because dotnet CLI is absent in this environment‚Äîneeds local runner/CI to confirm.    

  Steps                                                        

  1. Created worktree/branch fix/NX-03-issuance-500.           
  2. Updated IIssuanceService contract + implementation so publish/close log and return null when _db.Issuances.FindAsync misses, while preserving InvalidOperationException for bad states.                                                                   
  3. Simplified publish/close endpoints to call the service once and return NotFound when the nullable result indicates missing issuance.                                                                                                                      
  4. Attempted dotnet test ... but CLI isn‚Äôt installed here (dotnet: command not found); pushed branch after code review.      

  Table                                                        
  | Scope | Change | Reference |                               
  | --- | --- | --- |                                          
  | Service contract | PublishAsync/CloseAsync return Task<IssuanceResponse?>; log + return null when entity missing | services/issuance/Services/IssuanceService.cs:8 |                                                                                       
  | Publish endpoint | Single call to service, returns NotFound on null, keeps 400 for invalid states | services/issuance/Program.cs:228 |                                                                                                                     
  | Close endpoint | Same nullable handling path for /close | services/issuance/Program.cs:240 |                               
  | Logging | Added warnings for publish/close requests targeting nonexistent IDs | services/issuance/Services/IssuanceService.cs:63 |                                                                                                                         
  | Tests | Not run ‚Äì dotnet executable unavailable in this runtime | N/A |

  ### üöÄ –≠–¢–ê–ü 1: Merge & Cleanup (The Grand Merge)             

  –°–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ–º –≤—Å–µ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏ –≤ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—É—é –≤–µ—Ç–∫—É —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫–∏.  

  You are a Release Manager. Your goal is to merge all completed feature branches into `infra.defis.deploy`.                   

  **Context:**                                                 
  - Base branch: `infra.defis.deploy`.                         
  - Feature branches to merge:                                 
    - `origin/feature/NX-05-issuer-dashboard` (Issuer UI + Backend)                                                            
    - `origin/feature/NX-06-payout-schedule` (Spec Diff + Read-Only UI)                                                        
    - `origin/feature/NX-08-backoffice-audit` (Audit Log UI)   
    - `origin/fix/NX-03-issuance-500` (Issuance Bugfix)        
    - `origin/tasks/NX-01-spec-validate-and-matrix` (Docs + Specs)                                                             

  **Mission Plan:**                                            
  1.  **Go to main worktree:** `cd repositories/customer-gitlab/ois-cfa`.                                                      
  2.  **Checkout target:** `git checkout infra.defis.deploy`.  
  3.  **Pull latest:** `git pull origin infra.defis.deploy`.   
  4.  **Merge Loop:**                                          
      -   Merge `origin/tasks/NX-01-spec-validate-and-matrix`. 
      -   Merge `origin/fix/NX-03-issuance-500`.               
      -   Merge `origin/feature/NX-05-issuer-dashboard`.       
      -   Merge `origin/feature/NX-06-payout-schedule`.        
      -   Merge `origin/feature/NX-08-backoffice-audit`.       
      -   *Note:* If you encounter conflicts, resolve them intelligently (prefer incoming changes for UI/Docs, keep existing logic for Infra unless specified).                                                                                                
  5.  **Push:** `git push origin infra.defis.deploy`.          

  **Action:**                                                  
  - Perform the merges.                                        
  - Push the result.

‚Ä¢ TL;DR                                                        

  - Added artifacts/git/branch-zip-workflow.md outlining the ‚Äúzip‚Äù rationale, manual checklist, and operational policy; short file name makes it easy for the team to memorize the convention.                                                                 
  - Implemented scripts/git/zip_branches.sh + branch list artifacts/git/branch-zip-20251120.txt; script reads a txt file, checks merge status/worktrees, creates zip/<branch> tags, pushes, and deletes obsolete branches.                                     
  - Archived the merged branches (NX-01, NX-03, NX-05, NX-06, NX-08) by tagging + removing worktrees; submodule infra.defis.deploy updated and pushed.                                                                                                         

  Steps                                                        

  1. Documentation                                             
      - artifacts/git/branch-zip-workflow.md explains the pain point (‚Äúbranch cemetery‚Äù), why we prefer the short zip/ prefix, and the exact four-step manual flow. It also documents the helper script usage (./scripts/git/zip_branches.sh <list> [base]) and
        policy (‚Äúzip immediately after merging, don‚Äôt delete zip tags‚Äù).                                                       
  2. Automation                                                
      - Created executable scripts/git/zip_branches.sh: for each branch listed in a txt file it fetches refs, ensures the branch is ancestor of infra.defis.deploy, removes a clean worktree, tags zip/<branch>, pushes the tag, deletes remote/local branches.
      - Snapshot of branches that needed archiving recorded in artifacts/git/branch-zip-20251120.txt.                          
  3. Applied to merged branches                                
      - Ran the script on tasks/NX-01-spec-validate-and-matrix, fix/NX-03-issuance-500, tasks/NX-05-issuer-dashboard-and-reports, feature/NX-06-payout-schedule, feature/NX-08-backoffice-audit.                                                               
      - Worktrees for NX01/NX05/NX08/FIX03 were removed automatically; tags zip/<branch> pushed; remote branches deleted. (feature/NX-07-backoffice-kyc worktree intentionally kept since it‚Äôs still active.)                                                  

  Next actions                                                 

  1. Share the new doc/script with the team so everyone zips branches as soon as they merge into infra.defis.deploy.           
  2. When the next batch of branches is merged, update a txt list and rerun ./scripts/git/zip_branches.sh to keep the repo clean.

    64  ## Best practices
